For the following examples we will be using person_id = 31 (Tom Hanks) or person_id = 1 (George Lucas)

All examples are GET requests to http://localhost:5000/app/
You can find the results of the queries after the curl examples

================================== CURL EXAMPLES ================================== 

---------- person-id-from-name ------------
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/person-id-from-name?name=Tom%20Hanks
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/person-id-from-name?name=George%20Lucas


---------- QUERY 1 ------------
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query1?id=1

---------- QUERY 2 ------------
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query2-director?id=31
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query2-writer?id=1
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query2-producer?id=31

---------- QUERY 3 ------------
curl -X GET 'http://localhost:5000/app/query3?id=31&from=1990-05-05&to=2020-12-04'

---------- QUERY 4 ------------
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query4-original?id=31
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query4-spoken?id=31

---------- QUERY 5 ------------
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query5?k=5

---------- QUERY 6 ------------
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query6-budget?k=5
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query6-revenue?k=5

---------- QUERY 7 ------------
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query7?year=1995

---------- QUERY 8 ------------
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query8?year=1995

---------- QUERY 9 ------------
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query9?year=1995

---------- QUERY 11 ------------

---------- QUERY 14 ------------

---------- QUERY 15 ------------
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query15

---------- QUERY 16 ------------
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query16-best
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query16-worst

---------- QUERY 17 ------------
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query17-best
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query17-worst

---------- QUERY 18 ------------
curl -X GET http://localhost:5000/app/query18

!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
Because query 18 takes forever to execute, I will provide
results for a narrowed down version which is the last query
in the queries.txt file. I did not create a GET method
for this version of the query.
!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
